', Official Description (provided by the hotel)', 
', 
', Grand Hyatt Mumbai is located in the centre of Mumbai, India. More than a hotel, it is a multi-dimensional lifestyle complex located just 10 minutes from Mumbai\u2019s domestic airport and 20 minutes from the international airport and in close proximity to Bandra-Kurla complex, Mumbai\u2019s rapidly developing business district. The hotel features luxurious accommodation, contemporary serviced apartments, dining & entertainment options, spa, recreation & fitness facilities, conference & exhibition spaces & an international shopping plaza.',

ta.store('friendAvatarSwitcherObj', (function() {
var AVATAR_CLASS_GUID_REGEX = /\bavatarGUID:(\w+)\b/; // Class that contains the GUID of the member
//  whose avatar it's on.
var AVATAR_CLASS = 'potentialFacebookAvatar';         // Signal class for Mootools parsing of the DOM.
var AVATAR_CLASS_SELECTOR = '.' + AVATAR_CLASS;       // Selector needed for Mootools $$ function.
var guidToImgMap = {};        // mapping of member guids to avatar img tags
var friendGuidToSrcMap = {};  // mapping of friend guids* to facebook profile pic src values
//  *only ever contains guids of people with avatar img tags on page
var friendGuids = [];         // array of friend guids*, used because IE doesn't like for-each loops
//  *only ever contains guids of people with avatar img tags on page
return {
// Finds all avatars on the page that match the signal class, and stores them
// in a map for later replacement.
findAvatarsOnPage: function() {
$$(AVATAR_CLASS_SELECTOR).each(function (avatarImg) {
var guid = avatarImg.className.match(AVATAR_CLASS_GUID_REGEX);
if (guid && guid[1]) { // based on how JS regex works, guid[1] is the user's guid
guidToImgMap[guid[1]] = avatarImg; // associate the guid with the img tag
}
});
},
// Replaces all avatars on the page with the correct FB avatars, using
// the maps of GUIDs to img tags and FB profile src values.
replaceAvatarsOnPage: function() {
for (var i = 0; i < friendGuids.length; i++) { // because IE doesn't like for-each loops
var avatarImg = guidToImgMap[friendGuids[i]]
avatarImg.src = friendGuidToSrcMap[friendGuids[i]];
avatarImg.className = avatarImg.className.replace(AVATAR_CLASS_GUID_REGEX, '').replace(AVATAR_CLASS, '');
}
},
// Checks if guid is already in map of avatar img guids, and
// if it is, adds it to map of guids to be converted. This is called
// by a different file, such as friends_avatar_data_js.vm.
checkAndAddGuidAndSrc: function(guid, src) {
if (guidToImgMap.hasOwnProperty(guid)) {
friendGuids.push(guid);
friendGuidToSrcMap[guid] = src;
}
}
}
})());

}
ta.keep('facebook.data.onAvail.FRIEND_AVATARS', function() {
ta.retrieve('friendAvatarSwitcherObj').replaceAvatarsOnPage();
});
ta.queueForLoad(function() { // just in case we have the ta object before the DOM is fully initialized
ta.retrieve('friendAvatarSwitcherObj').findAvatarsOnPage(); // as soon as we can, start parsing the DOM for avatars
}, "findAvatarsOnPage");

function daysSince(curr, prev) {
var current = new Date(curr.getFullYear(), curr.getMonth(), curr.getDate());
var previous = new Date(prev.getFullYear(), prev.getMonth(), prev.getDate());
var timeSince = current.getTime() - previous.getTime();
var days = timeSince / 86400000; // 86400000 milliseconds = 1 day
return Math.floor(days);
}
function isChromePluginInstalled(extensionId, installedCallback, notInstalledCallback)
{
if (chrome && chrome.runtime && chrome.runtime.sendMessage) {
chrome.runtime.sendMessage(extensionId, { message: "installed" },
function (reply) {
if (reply) {
installedCallback && installedCallback();
} else {
notInstalledCallback && notInstalledCallback();
}
}
);
} else {
notInstalledCallback();
}
}
function requestPcbVelocity(placement) {
var reqData = {
servletClass: "MetaPlacementAjax",
placementName: placement,
assets: "false",
wrap: "true",
skipLocation: "true"
}
require(['overlays/Overlay', 'overlays/styles/modal', 'overlays/position', 'overlays/options/closeOnEscape',
'overlays/options/closeOnDocClick', 'overlays/options/autoReposition', 'overlays/styles/windowshade',
'overlays/options/ajax'],
function(Overlay, Modal, Position, CloseOnEscape, CloseOnDocClick, AutoReposition, WindowShade, Ajax) {
var pcb = new Overlay(null, [
Modal(null, 'center', 'pcb', '', '', null),
Position.center([0,0]),
CloseOnEscape,
CloseOnDocClick,
AutoReposition,
WindowShade(),
Ajax('/MetaPlacementAjax', {reqParams:reqData, resources:["https://static.tacdn.com/css2/pcb_branding_interstitial_rollout_p1-v23821076790b.css"]})
]);
pcb.on('hide', function(target) {
var hideType;
if (target.trigger) {
if (target.trigger == 'doc-click') {
hideType = 'booking_interstitial' + '_exit_outside';
}
else if (target.trigger == 'close-button') {
hideType = 'booking_interstitial' + '_exit_x';
}
else {
hideType = 'booking_interstitial' + '_exit_button';
}
}
ta.remove("PCBInterstitialOpen");
ta.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign', hideType || 'booking_interstitial' + '_exit_outside', "Hotel_Review", null, true);
}).on('contentLoaded', function() {
ta.trackEventOnPage('interruption_record', 'popup', 'pcb_campaign_interstitial', 0, true);
ta.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign', 'popup', 'pcb_campaign_interstitial', 0, true);
var closeButton = ta.find('.ui_button', pcb.container);
closeButton && closeButton.addEvent('click', function(e) {
pcb.hide();
});
});
pcb.show();
ta.store("PCBInterstitialOpen", true);
setTimeout(function() {
if (pcb && pcb.isOpen()) {
ta.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign', 'booking_interstitial' + '_in_view', "Hotel_Review", null, true);
}
}, 3000);
}
);
}

});
}, 200);
}, 'load the pcb interstitial')

function ip_adjustHeader() {
// check for overlap
var prefs = ta.id('USER_PREFS');
var head = ta.id('HEAD');
if (!prefs || !head) {
return;
}
var logo = head.getElement('.topLogo');
if (logo) {
var c = prefs.getCoordinates();
if (c.left - logo.getCoordinates().right < 10) {
head.setStyle('padding-top', 5);
}
}
}

define("booking/common/ChildAgesSerialization", [],
function(){
var AGES_SEPARATOR = ',';
var ROOMS_SEPARATOR = ':';
var DESERIALIZE_REGEX = new RegExp(AGES_SEPARATOR+'|'+ROOMS_SEPARATOR);
function _deserializeChildren(childrenAgesStr) {
if (childrenAgesStr == null || childrenAgesStr.length == 0) {
return [];
}
return childrenAgesStr.split(DESERIALIZE_REGEX).map(function (el) {return parseInt(el,10);}).filter(function(n){return !isNaN(n);});
}
function _serializeChildren(rooms,childrenAges) {
if (childrenAges == null || childrenAges.length == 0) {
return '';
}
var childrenPerRoom = Math.floor(childrenAges.length/rooms);
var extraChildren = childrenAges.length - (childrenPerRoom * rooms);
var roomStrings = [];
var nextIndex = 0;
for (var i = 0 ; i < rooms ; ++i) {
var childrenInRoom = 0;
if (i < extraChildren) {
childrenInRoom = childrenPerRoom + 1;
} else {
childrenInRoom = childrenPerRoom;
}
if (childrenInRoom) {
var endIndex = Math.min(nextIndex + childrenInRoom, childrenAges.length);
var inRoom = childrenAges.slice(nextIndex, endIndex);
nextIndex = endIndex;
roomStrings.push(inRoom.join(AGES_SEPARATOR));
}
}
return roomStrings.join(ROOMS_SEPARATOR);
}
return {
deserialize: _deserializeChildren,
serialize: _serializeChildren
}

// Age pickers
//
//update picker text and status of a specific age picker to given age
// @param age - the new age to show
// @param agePicker - the picker to update
function _selectAgeForPicker(age, agePicker, showError) {
var error=false;
//this means age was not selected yet
if (age === -1) {
age = 'Age';//{@localize key="mem_pf_928"/} {! Age !}
error = true;
}
if (age === 0) {
age = '0-1';
}
api.find('.picker-inner .picker-label', agePicker).firstChild.nodeValue = age;
api.find('.curoption .picker-label', agePicker).firstChild.nodeValue = age;
if (!error || !showError) {
api.removeClass(api.find('.picker-inner', agePicker), 'error');
} else {
api.addClass(api.find('.picker-inner', agePicker), 'error');
}
//for removing the age-error text
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_agesPopupVerify();
} else {
_updateAgesErrorMsg(true);
}
}
//adds event listener for a specific age picker dropdown option
// @param option - the drop down element
// @param age - the age it represents
// @param agePicker - the picker adding to
function _addSelectAgeListener(option, age, agePicker) {
api.addEvent(option, 'click', function(event) {
_selectAgeForPicker(age, agePicker, true);
_showPicker(false, agePicker);
_updateGuestsRoomsObject();
event.stopPropagation();
});
}
//adds age option to a specific picker
// @param age - the age to add
// @param agePicker - the picker to add to
// @param optionsParent - the dropdown options parent element
function _addAgeToPicker(age, agePicker, optionsParent){
var option = new Element('li');
api.addClass(option,'option');
option.setContent(age);
_addSelectAgeListener(option, age, agePicker);
optionsParent.appendChild(option);
}
//fills the given age picker dropdown with age options
function _fillAges(agePicker) {
var optionsParent = api.find(' .picker-dropdown .options-container', agePicker);
_addAgeToPicker('0-1', agePicker, optionsParent);
for (var i = 1 ; i <= MAX_CHILD_AGE ; ++i ) {
_addAgeToPicker("" + i, agePicker, optionsParent);
}
}
// fill the given age picker  and add it to dom
function _addAgePicker(agePicker, index) {
var childLocArr = ta.retrieve('rgPicker.nChildIndex'), // Child {0}
childStr = childLocArr && childLocArr.length > index ? childLocArr[index] : '';
var id = 'age-picker-' + index;
agePicker.id = id; //id should be enough, but ta.find does not work properly with id selector, so adding class as well
api.addClass(agePicker, id);
api.setStyle(agePicker, 'order', index); //make sure they are laid out in the correct order
var titleElement = api.find('.picker-title', agePicker);
titleElement.innerHTML = childStr;
api.addEvent(agePicker, 'click', function(event) {
_togglePicker(agePicker);
_flushScrollbar(agePicker);
event.stopPropagation();
});
_fillAges(agePicker);
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_agesPickerContainerElement.insertBefore(agePicker, _popupUpdateButton);
} else {
_agesPickerContainerElement.appendChild(agePicker);
}
}
//updates the number of age pickers according to given number of children
function _createAgePickers(nChildren, show) {
var agePicker
, i
;
//remove unneeded pickers
for (i = nChildren ; i < MAX_CHILDREN ; ++i) {
agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
if (!agePicker) {
break;
}
_agesPickerContainerElement.removeChild(agePicker);
}
for (i = 0 ; i < nChildren ; ++i) {
agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
if (agePicker) {
continue;
}
var newPicker = _agePickerTemplate.cloneNode(true);
api.removeClass(newPicker, 'hidden');
api.removeClass(newPicker, 'age-picker-template');
_addAgePicker(newPicker, (i + 1));
}
if (nChildren > 0) {
api.removeClass(_childrenAgesExplain, 'hidden');
}
else {
api.addClass(_childrenAgesExplain, 'hidden');
}
if (show && (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup)) {
_showAgePickersPopup(true, nChildren > 0);
}
}
//create age pickers with given ages
// @param childrenAges - array of age values (integer, 0-17)
function _createAgePickersWithAges(childrenAges, showErrors) {
_createAgePickers(childrenAges.length, false);
for( var i = 0 ; i < childrenAges.length ; ++i) {
var agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
_selectAgeForPicker(childrenAges[i], agePicker, showErrors);
}
}
//collects the children ages from all pickers.
// @returns - array of ages, -1 if age not selected
function _gatherChildrenAges() {
var ages = [];
for( var i = 0 ; i < MAX_CHILDREN ; ++i) {
var agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
if (!agePicker) {
break;
}
var age = parseInt(api.find('.picker-inner .picker-label', agePicker).firstChild.nodeValue, 10);
if (isNaN(age)) {
ages.push(-1);
} else {
ages.push(age);
}
}
return ages;
}
function _showAgesAsText(asText) {
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
_childrenAges = ages;
if (asText) {
var agesStrings = ages.map(function(a) { return a === 0 ? '0-1' : a; });
_childrenAgesText.innerHTML = ': ' + agesStrings.join(',') + ' ';
api.removeClass(_childrenAgesText, 'hidden');
api.removeClass(_childrenAgesChange, 'hidden');
} else if (!_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
api.addClass(_childrenAgesText, 'hidden');
api.addClass(_childrenAgesChange, 'hidden');
}
if (!_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
for (var i = 0; i < MAX_CHILDREN; ++i) {
var agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
if (!agePicker) {
break;
}
if (asText) {
api.addClass(agePicker, 'hidden');
} else {
api.removeClass(agePicker, 'hidden');
}
}
}
}
function _showAgePickersInlinePopup() {
api.addClass(_agesWrapElement, 'selecting');
api.addEvent(document, 'click', _onHidePopup);
}
function _hideAgePickersInlinePopup() {
if (_agesPopupVerify()) {
api.removeClass(_agesWrapElement, 'selecting');
_showAgesAsText(true);
api.removeEvent(document, 'click', _onHidePopup);
}
}
function _showAgePickersPopup(show, hasAges) {
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
if (show && hasAges) {
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_agesPopupVerify();
api.addClass(_agesWrapElement, 'hidden');
if (!_childAgePickersPopup) {
_agesPopupInit();
}
_childAgePickersPopup.show();
_mainOverlaysArr.forEach(function (o) {
o.hide();
});
}
else if (_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
_showAgePickersInlinePopup();
}
} else if(hasAges) {
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
api.removeClass(_agesWrapElement, 'hidden');
}
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
} else {
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
api.addClass(_agesWrapElement, 'hidden');
}
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
}
}
// general
//
function _fillPickerOptions(parent, labelsName, min, max, prop, triggerSearchFirstOption, triggerSearchAll) {
var optionsParent = api.find(' .picker-dropdown .options-container', parent)
, labels = ta.retrieve(labelsName)
, option
, obj
, i
;
for ( i = min ; i <= max ; ++i ) {
option = new Element('li');
api.addClass(option, 'option');
option.setContent(labels[i]);
obj = {};
obj[prop] = i;
_addPickerListener(parent, option, obj, triggerSearchAll || (triggerSearchFirstOption && i === min));
optionsParent.appendChild(option);
}
}
function _addPickerListener(picker, option, values, triggerSearch) {
api.addEvent(option, 'click', function(event) {
var changed = _updateValues(values, true, true);
_showPicker(false, picker);
_verifyFields(false, false, true);
event.stopPropagation();
if (triggerSearch && changed) {
_doSearch(false, event);
}
});
}
function _togglePicker(parent, trk) {
//this is an overlay...
var willShow;
if (parent && parent.isOpen) {
willShow = !parent.isOpen();
} else {
var dropdown = api.find('.picker-dropdown', parent);
willShow = api.hasClass(dropdown, 'hidden');
}
_showPicker(willShow, parent);
if (trk && willShow) {
_trackEvent(trk);
}
}
function _hideChildAgePickersPopup(){
if (_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
_hideAgePickersInlinePopup();
}
else if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && _childAgePickersPopup && _childAgePickersPopup.isOpen()) {
_childAgePickersPopup.hide();
}
}
function _showPicker(show, parent) {
//close a picker if already open
var currentlyOpenDD = api.find('.picker-dropdown:not(.hidden)', _widgetDiv);
if (parent.isOpen) {
api.addClass(currentlyOpenDD, 'hidden');
if(show) {
if(!parent.isOpen()) {
_mainOverlaysArr.forEach(function(o) { o.hide(); });
}
parent.show();
//close the ages popup in case one of the main pickers is opened
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
} else {
parent.hide();
}
} else {
_mainOverlaysArr.forEach(function(o) { o.hide(); });
var dropdown = api.find('.picker-dropdown', parent);
if (currentlyOpenDD !== dropdown) {
api.addClass(currentlyOpenDD, 'hidden');
}
if (api.hasClass(dropdown, 'hidden')) {
if (show) {
api.removeClass(dropdown, 'hidden');
}
} else {
if (!show) {
api.addClass(dropdown, 'hidden');
}
}
//close the ages popup in case one of the main pickers is opened
if (show && (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) && (!api.hasClass(parent, 'age-picker'))) {
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
}
}
//one place to hold logic for all versions of the test
function _updateValues(valuesObj, show, notify) {
var nRooms = valuesObj.nRooms || _numRooms
, nAdults = valuesObj.nAdults || _numAdults
, nChildren = (typeof(valuesObj.nChildren) === 'undefined' ? _numChildren : valuesObj.nChildren)
, newNumAdults
, newNumChildren
, newNumRooms;
if (_numRooms === nRooms && _numAdults === nAdults && _numChildren === nChildren) {
return false;
}
if (nRooms !== _numRooms) {
newNumRooms = nRooms;
if (newNumRooms > nAdults) {
//at least one adult per room
newNumAdults = newNumRooms;
} else {
//no more then 4 adults per room
newNumAdults = Math.min(nRooms * MAX_ADULTS_PER_ROOM, nAdults);
}
//no more then 8 children per room.
newNumChildren = Math.min(nRooms * MAX_CHILDREN_PER_ROOM, nChildren);
} else {
//minimal number of rooms as dictated by number of adults
var adultsRequiredNumberOfRooms = Math.ceil(nAdults / MAX_ADULTS_PER_ROOM);
//but they might want more rooms
adultsRequiredNumberOfRooms = Math.max(adultsRequiredNumberOfRooms, nRooms);
//minimal number of rooms as dictated by number of children
var childrenRequiredNumberOfRooms = Math.ceil(nChildren / MAX_CHILDREN_PER_ROOM);
//maximal number of rooms required
newNumRooms = Math.max(adultsRequiredNumberOfRooms, childrenRequiredNumberOfRooms);
//at least one adult per room
newNumRooms = Math.min(newNumRooms, nAdults);
//force max children per room
newNumChildren = Math.min(nChildren, newNumRooms * MAX_CHILDREN_PER_ROOM);
newNumAdults = nAdults;
}
var changed = false;
if (newNumRooms !== _numRooms) {
_setRoomsLabel(newNumRooms);
changed = true;
}
if (newNumChildren !== _numChildren) {
_createAgePickers(newNumChildren, show);
}
if (newNumAdults !== _numAdults) {
_setAdultsLabel(newNumAdults);
changed = true;
}
if (newNumChildren !== _numChildren) {
_setChildrenLabel(newNumChildren);
changed = true;
}
_numRooms = newNumRooms;
_numAdults = newNumAdults;
_numChildren = newNumChildren;
if (notify) {
_updateGuestsRoomsObject(false);
}
return changed;
}
//handle click outside of the drop downs of the various pickers
function _closeOpenPicker(event) {
var openDD = api.find('.picker-dropdown:not(.hidden)', _widgetDiv);
api.addClass(openDD, 'hidden');
_mainOverlaysArr.forEach(function(o) {
if (!event || !o.sourceElement.contains(event.target)) {
o.hide();
}
});
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
if(!event || event.target !== _childrenAgesChange) {
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
}
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
}
function _trackEvent(action) {
var trackingTree = '',
ik = ta.retrieve("tracking.impression.key"),
locationId = ta.retrieve('page.location');
if (ik) {
trackingTree =  "IK:" + ik;
}
if (locationId) {
trackingTree += "/L:" + locationId;
}
var context = _dynamicContext ? _detectContext() : _trackContext;
ta.trackEventOnPage('GuestSelector-'+context||'', action, trackingTree, "1", false);
}
//updates the global object with selected values
function _updateGuestsRoomsObject() {
var orig = ta.retrieve('guests.rooms.object');
var obj = {
guests:_numAdults,
rooms:_numRooms,
child_rm_ages: ser.serialize(_numRooms, _gatherChildrenAges())
};
var changed = JSON.stringify(orig) !== JSON.stringify(obj);
var curDates = JSON.stringify(_calendarProxy.getDates());
if(!changed )
{
changed = _lastKnownDates !== curDates;
}
_lastKnownDates = curDates;
if (changed) {
ta.store('guests.rooms.object', obj);
_setDirtyMode(true);
//let other children pickers know about the new values
ta.fireEvent('onLegacyGuestsChanged', obj);
if (_childAgePickersPopup) {
_childAgePickersPopup.reposition();
}
}
}
function _onSearchFieldsChanged(source){
if (source === _widgetDiv){
return;
}
var obj = ta.retrieve('guests.rooms.object');
_childrenAges = ser.deserialize(obj.child_rm_ages);
_createAgePickersWithAges(_childrenAges, false);
_setInitialState(obj.rooms, obj.guests, false);
_showAgesAsText(true);
}
function _onClearSearch() {
_updateValues( {nRooms:1, nAdults:2, nChildren:0}, true, true );
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup ) {
api.addClass(_widgetDiv, 'hidden');
}
}
function _setDirtyMode(dirty) {
_dirty = dirty;
if (_calendarProxy.hasDates()) {
if (_searchButton && _canChangeSearchButton) {
if (!_showChildrenAgesInPopup && !api.hasClass(_searchButton,'no_hide')) {
_searchButton.firstChild.nodeValue = ta.retrieve('common_update_results');//"Update Results";
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'original');
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'primary');
} else if(_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
var inner = api.find('.change_dates_text', _searchButton);
(inner || _searchButton).firstChild.nodeValue = ta.retrieve('airm_updateSearchLabel');//"Update Search";
}
}
}
if (dirty) {
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
if (!api.hasClass(_searchButton, 'no_hide')) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'hidden');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && (!_childAgePickersPopup || !_childAgePickersPopup.isOpen())) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup && !api.hasClass(_agesWrapElement, 'selecting')) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
_showAgesAsText(false);
} else {
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
if (!api.hasClass(_searchButton, 'no_hide')) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'hidden');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && (!_childAgePickersPopup || !_childAgePickersPopup.isOpen())) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup && !api.hasClass(_agesWrapElement, 'selecting')) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
_showAgesAsText(true);
}
}
function _updateAgesErrorMsg(removeOnly, hasAgesError) {
var hasErrors = false;
if (typeof(hasAgesError) === "undefined") {
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
for (var i = 0; i < ages.length; ++i) {
if (ages[i] < 0) {
hasErrors = true;
}
}
} else {
hasErrors = hasAgesError;
}
if (!hasErrors) {
api.addClass(api.find('.ages-error', _agesWrapElement), 'hidden');
} else if (!removeOnly) {
_trackEvent('age_validation_error');
api.removeClass(api.find('.ages-error', _agesWrapElement), 'hidden');
}
}
//verify fields values
// @params interactive - indicated if should show visuals on errors
// @returns - boolean indicating if error was found
function _verifyFields(interactive, agesOnly, removeAgesErrorIsPossible) {
var hasErrors = false,
hasAgesError = false;
if (!_calendarProxy.hasDates()) {
if (interactive) {
_calendarProxy.showCalendar();
}
hasErrors = true;
}
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
for (var i = 0 ; i < ages.length ; ++i) {
if (ages[i] < 0) {
hasErrors = true;
hasAgesError = true;
if (interactive || agesOnly) {
api.addClass(api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1) + ' .picker-inner', _agesPickerContainerElement), 'error');
}
}
}
if (interactive || agesOnly) {
_updateAgesErrorMsg(false, hasAgesError);
}
if (removeAgesErrorIsPossible && !hasAgesError) {
api.addClass(api.find('.ages-error', _agesWrapElement), 'hidden');
}
return !hasErrors;
}
function _agesPopupVerify() {
var hasAgesError = false;
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
for (var i = 0 ; i < ages.length ; ++i) {
if (ages[i] < 0) {
hasAgesError = true;
break;
}
}
if (!hasAgesError) {
api.removeClass(_popupUpdateButton, 'disabled');
} else {
api.addClass(_popupUpdateButton, 'disabled');
}
return !hasAgesError;
}
function _updateSearchButtonPopupClick(event) {
if (_agesPopupVerify()) {
_showAgesAsText(true);
_showAgePickersPopup(false, _childrenAges.length > 0);
if (!_searchImmediately) { //search immediatly will trigger the search from the hide popup function, so no need to do this again
_doSearch(true, event);
}
}
}
function _doSearch(triggerDatesSelected, event) {
_closeOpenPicker();
if (!_verifyFields(true) && _canChangeSearchButton) {
return;
}
if (triggerDatesSelected && _canChangeSearchButton) {
var dates = _calendarProxy.getDates();
_calendarProxy.fireDatesChanged(dates);
}
if (typeof(_origSearchHandler) === 'function') {
_origSearchHandler.apply(_searchButton,[event]);
}
_setDirtyMode(false);
ta.fireEvent('searchFieldsChanged', _widgetDiv);
}
function _changeAgesClick(event) {
if(event) {
event.stopPropagation();
}
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
_showAgePickersPopup(true, true);
}
if (!_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_showAgesAsText(false);
}
_trackEvent('change_age_click');
}
//search button click handler
function _searchClick(event) {
event = new Event(event);
event.stop();
_trackEvent('update_results_click');
_doSearch(true, event);
}
function _onDatesChanged(sourceElement, type) {
if (! _calendarProxy.isDateTypeRelevant(type)) {
return;
}
if (api.hasClass(sourceElement, 'prw_ibex_rooms_guests_picker')  //triggered by one of the instances of this widget
|| _closestDatePickers.indexOf(sourceElement) === -1) { //triggered by a date picker of other instance
//need to hide search button
_setDirtyMode(false);
return;
}
if (!_noAutoHac) {
//search immediately when dates changed
_doSearch(false);
//show after search started. needed for the way hotels page works
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && _calendarProxy.hasDates()) {
setTimeout(function () {
api.removeClass(_widgetDiv, 'hidden');
}, 100);
}
}
}
// somewhat similar to the one in Desktop.js, but can get which picker type
function _findClosestDatepicker(type) {
var el,
target = _widgetDiv;
while (target && target !== document.body) {
el = target.getElement('[data-dateType='+type+']');
if (el) {
return el;
}
target = target.parentNode;
}
return null;
}
function _findSearchButton()
{
// looking for the relevant search button - it is located outside of the widget
// since it is implemented by the container that uses the widget.
// but this should not be too far away, so looking two levels up max.
var parent = _widgetDiv.parentNode;
for (var i = 0 ; i < 2 ; ++i) {
var button = api.find('.update_results_button', parent);
if (button) {
return button;
}
parent = parent.parentNode;
}
return null;
}
function _detectContext() {
var classStr = _widgetDiv.className.toLowerCase(),
classArray = classStr.split(' ').filter(function(s) { return s.indexOf('wctx-',0) === 0; });
if (classArray.length > 0) {
return classArray[0].substring(5);
}
}
function _commonInit() {
_searchImmediately = api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'popup_with_button');
_showChildrenAgesInPopup = _searchImmediately || api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'popup');
_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup = api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'inline_popup');
_noAutoHac = api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'noAutoHac');
_dynamicContext = api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'dynamic_context');
_trackContext = _detectContext();
_agesWrapElement = api.find('.ages-wrap', _widgetDiv);
_agesPickerContainerElement = _showChildrenAgesInPopup ? api.find('.ages-wrap-popup-container', _widgetDiv) : _agesWrapElement;
_agePickerTemplate = api.find('.ages-wrap .age-picker-template', _widgetDiv);
_initialValuesHolder = api.find('.initial-values-holder', _widgetDiv);
_childrenAgesExplain = api.find('.children-ages-explain', _widgetDiv);
_childrenAgesChange = api.find('.ages_change', _childrenAgesExplain);
_childrenAgesText = api.find('.ages_text', _childrenAgesExplain);
_searchButton = _findSearchButton();
_canChangeSearchButton = ! api.hasClass(_searchButton,'no_change');
_numRooms = Number(_initialValuesHolder.getAttribute('numRooms'));
_numAdults = Number(_initialValuesHolder.getAttribute('numAdults'));
_childrenAgesStr = _initialValuesHolder.getAttribute('childrenAges');
_closestDatePickers = [_findClosestDatepicker('CHECKIN'), _findClosestDatepicker('CHECKOUT')];
if (_searchButton) {
_origSearchHandler = _searchButton.onclick;
_searchButton.onclick = _searchClick;
}
_childrenAgesChange.onclick = _changeAgesClick;
_calendarProxy.onDatesSelected(_onDatesChanged);
ta.on('searchFieldsChanged', _onSearchFieldsChanged);
ta.on('childrenClearSearch', _onClearSearch);
_childrenAges = ser.deserialize(_childrenAgesStr);
_createAgePickersWithAges(_childrenAges, true);
api.addEvent(document, 'click', _closeOpenPicker);
_lastKnownDates = JSON.stringify(_calendarProxy.getDates());
}
function _flushScrollbar(parentElement) {
if(!parentElement) {
return;
}
var scrollContainer = api.find('.options-container', parentElement);
if(!scrollContainer) {
return;
}
//on mac, this will animate the scroll bar so the user knows it can be scrolled
scrollContainer.scrollTop = scrollContainer.scrollTop + 1;
scrollContainer.scrollTop = scrollContainer.scrollTop - 1;
}
function _pickerClick(event, pickerElement, overlay, pickerTrack) {
if (!overlay) {
overlay = _setupDropdown(pickerElement, pickerTrack);
_mainOverlaysArr.push(overlay);
}
_togglePicker(overlay, pickerTrack);
_flushScrollbar(api.find('.picker-dropdown', overlay.container));
return overlay;
}
function _setupDropdown(pickerElement, pickerTrack) {
var dropdown = null;
var content = api.find('.picker-dropdown', pickerElement);
api.removeClass(content, 'hidden');
var size = api.getSize(pickerElement);
var dropdownStyle = 'border: 1px solid #589442;border-radius: 3px;padding:0;';
dropdown = new Overlay(
pickerElement,
Dropdown(pickerElement, 'below', [_widgetDiv.get('class')], content, dropdownStyle, 'div'),
Position.below([0, -(size.y || 36)]),
MatchWidth && MatchWidth(pickerElement),
CloseOnDocClick,
CloseOnLegacyOverlay,
CloseOnTargetEvent(window, ['date_bar_docked', 'date_bar_undocked'])
);
api.removeClass(dropdown.contentElement, 'hidden');
api.find('.curoption', dropdown.container).onclick = function(event) {
_togglePicker(dropdown, pickerTrack);
_flushScrollbar(content);
event.stopPropagation();
};
return dropdown;
}
function _hrInit() {
_roomsElement = api.find('.rooms-picker .unified-picker', _widgetDiv);
_adultsElement = api.find('.adults-picker .unified-picker', _widgetDiv);
_childrenElement = api.find('.children-picker .unified-picker', _widgetDiv);
_fillRoomsOptions();
_fillAdultsOptions();
_fillChildrenOptions();
_roomsElement.onclick = function(event) { _roomsOverlay = _pickerClick(event, _roomsElement, _roomsOverlay, 'room_picker_open'); };
_adultsElement.onclick = function(event) { _adultsOverlay = _pickerClick(event, _adultsElement, _adultsOverlay, 'adult_picker_open'); };
_childrenElement.onclick = function(event) { _childrenOverlay = _pickerClick(event, _childrenElement, _childrenOverlay, 'children_picker_open'); };
}
function _onHidePopup() {
//remove children which for age was not picked.
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
ages = ages.filter(function(a){ return a >= 0; });
_updateValues({nChildren:ages.length}, true, true);
_createAgePickersWithAges(ages, false);
_showAgesAsText(true);
_showAgePickersPopup(false, ages.length > 0);
if (_dirty) {
_doSearch(false);
}
}
function _agesPopupInit() {
_popupUpdateButton = api.find('.update_search_button', _agesPickerContainerElement );
_popupUpdateButton.onclick = _updateSearchButtonPopupClick;
if (_searchImmediately) {
api.removeClass(_popupUpdateButton, 'hidden');
}
api.removeClass(_agesPickerContainerElement, 'hidden');
_childAgePickersPopup = new Overlay(
_childrenElement,
Tooltip(_childrenElement, 'below', [_widgetDiv.get('class')], _agesPickerContainerElement, 'div'),
Position.below(),
CloseOnDocClick,
CloseOnLegacyOverlay,
CloseOnTargetEvent(window, ['date_bar_docked', 'date_bar_undocked'])
);
api.removeClass(_childAgePickersPopup.container,'hidden');
_childAgePickersPopup.on('hide', _onHidePopup);
}
//init the components with given rooms/adults/children values.
function _setInitialState(nRooms, nAdults, notify) {
_updateValues({ nRooms:nRooms || _numRooms, nAdults:nAdults || _numAdults, nChildren:_childrenAges.length }, false, notify);
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_showAgePickersPopup(false, _childrenAges.length > 0);
}
if (_verifyFields(false)) {
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
if (!api.hasClass(_searchButton, 'no_hide')) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'hidden');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
_showAgesAsText(true);
} else {
_showAgesAsText(false);
}
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && !api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'no_hide')) {
if (_calendarProxy.hasDates()) {
api.removeClass(_widgetDiv, 'hidden');
} else {
api.addClass(_widgetDiv, 'hidden');
}
}
}
function _setupCalendarProxy() {
if (ta.page && ta.page.getDates) {
_calendarProxy = {
hasDates: function() { return ta.page.hasDates('STAYDATES'); },
getDates: function() { return ta.page.getDates('STAYDATES'); },
showCalendar: function() { ta.page.gatherDatesNear(event.target, null, false); },
fireDatesChanged: function(dates) { ta.page.onDatesSelected(_closestDatePickers[0], 'STAYDATES', dates, true); },
onDatesSelected: function(callback) { ta.page.on('dateSelected', callback); },
isDateTypeRelevant: function(type) { return type === 'STAYDATES'; }
};
} else if(ta.widgets && ta.widgets.calendar) {
_calendarProxy = {
hasDates: function() { return ta.widgets.calendar.hasPageDates(); },
getDates: function() { return ta.widgets.calendar.getDateArgsObject(); },
showCalendar: function() { },
fireDatesChanged: function(/* dates */) { ta.widgets.calendar.updateSDCalendar(); },
onDatesSelected: function(callback) { ta.on('onCalendarRangeSelect', callback); },
isDateTypeRelevant: function(/* type */) { return true; }
};
}
}
//init the widget
function _init(){
_setupCalendarProxy();
_commonInit();
if (ta.retrieve('feature.CHILDREN_SEARCH'))
{
_hrInit();
}
if (ta.retrieve('guests.rooms.object')) {
//this is a widget refresh, take values from ta to keep in sync with other instances
_onSearchFieldsChanged();
} else {
//this is the first render - take values from default fields
_setInitialState(null,null,true);
}
}
ta.queueForLoad(function() {
_init();
}, 'rooms and guests picker widget handlers');
});

(function(){
var define = ta.prwidgets.define.bind(ta.prwidgets,'datepickers_inline_calendar_datepicker','handlers.js');
define(['widget'], function(widget) {
'use strict';
var _checkinElement = ta.find('[data-datetype=CHECKIN]', widget.element)
, _checkoutElement = ta.find('[data-datetype=CHECKOUT]', widget.element)
;
function _setDateLabel(target, date) {
var label;
if (!date) {
label = target.getAttribute('data-emptyText');
} else {
// TODO: Should pull this out of CalendarUtil eventually
label = ta.widgets.calendar.dateToString(
date,
ta.widgets.calendar.getDatePickerFormat('classic')
);
}
ta.find('.picker-inner .picker-label', target).firstChild.nodeValue = label; /* HOT-4599 */
}
function _onDateSelected(target, dateType, date) {
// Clean up if the widget is no longer in the document.
if (!ta.inDocument(widget.element)) {
ta.page.removeListener('dateSelected', _onDateSelected);
_checkinElement = null;
_checkoutElement = null;
return;
}
if (dateType === 'CHECKIN') {
_setDateLabel(_checkinElement, date[0]);
} else if (dateType === 'CHECKOUT') {
_setDateLabel(_checkoutElement, date[0]);
} else if (dateType === 'STAYDATES') {
_setDateLabel(_checkinElement, date[0]);
_setDateLabel(_checkoutElement, date[1]);
}
}
/* HOT-4552 */
function _onDatePickerClick(elmt) {
if (!elmt) {
return;
}
var calendarFlyout = elmt.getParent(".calendarFlyout");
if (calendarFlyout) {
var deferred = calendarFlyout.retrieve('deferred'),
calendarWrapper = calendarFlyout.getElement('.calendarWrapper');
if (deferred && calendarWrapper) {
deferred.reject();
ta.page.gatherDates(elmt, calendarWrapper);
return;
}
}
ta.page.gatherDates(elmt);
}
ta.queueForLoad(function() {
ta.page.on('dateSelected', _onDateSelected);
}, 'datepicker widget handlers');
return {
onDatePickerClick: _onDatePickerClick
};
});})();

', Grand Hyatt Mumbai is located in the centre of Mumbai, India. More than a hotel, it is a multi-dimensional lifestyle complex located just 10 minutes from Mumbai\u2019s domestic airport and 20 minutes from the international airport and in close proximity to Bandra-Kurla complex, Mumbai\u2019s rapidly developing business district. The hotel features luxurious accommodation, contemporary serviced apartments, dining & entertainment options, spa, recreation & fitness facilities, conference & exhibition spaces & an international shopping plaza.',

ta.store('friendAvatarSwitcherObj', (function() {
var AVATAR_CLASS_GUID_REGEX = /\bavatarGUID:(\w+)\b/; // Class that contains the GUID of the member
//  whose avatar it's on.
var AVATAR_CLASS = 'potentialFacebookAvatar';         // Signal class for Mootools parsing of the DOM.
var AVATAR_CLASS_SELECTOR = '.' + AVATAR_CLASS;       // Selector needed for Mootools $$ function.
var guidToImgMap = {};        // mapping of member guids to avatar img tags
var friendGuidToSrcMap = {};  // mapping of friend guids* to facebook profile pic src values
//  *only ever contains guids of people with avatar img tags on page
var friendGuids = [];         // array of friend guids*, used because IE doesn't like for-each loops
//  *only ever contains guids of people with avatar img tags on page
return {
// Finds all avatars on the page that match the signal class, and stores them
// in a map for later replacement.
findAvatarsOnPage: function() {
$$(AVATAR_CLASS_SELECTOR).each(function (avatarImg) {
var guid = avatarImg.className.match(AVATAR_CLASS_GUID_REGEX);
if (guid && guid[1]) { // based on how JS regex works, guid[1] is the user's guid
guidToImgMap[guid[1]] = avatarImg; // associate the guid with the img tag
}
});
},
// Replaces all avatars on the page with the correct FB avatars, using
// the maps of GUIDs to img tags and FB profile src values.
replaceAvatarsOnPage: function() {
for (var i = 0; i < friendGuids.length; i++) { // because IE doesn't like for-each loops
var avatarImg = guidToImgMap[friendGuids[i]]
avatarImg.src = friendGuidToSrcMap[friendGuids[i]];
avatarImg.className = avatarImg.className.replace(AVATAR_CLASS_GUID_REGEX, '').replace(AVATAR_CLASS, '');
}
},
// Checks if guid is already in map of avatar img guids, and
// if it is, adds it to map of guids to be converted. This is called
// by a different file, such as friends_avatar_data_js.vm.
checkAndAddGuidAndSrc: function(guid, src) {
if (guidToImgMap.hasOwnProperty(guid)) {
friendGuids.push(guid);
friendGuidToSrcMap[guid] = src;
}
}
}
})());
// Make the partial request, and set our response behavior.
ta.merge('facebook.data.params', {uid: '748968D3955EE94B629CA2547F620B0A'});          if(ta.keep) {
ta.keep('facebook.data.request', 'FRIEND_AVATARS');
}
ta.keep('facebook.data.onAvail.FRIEND_AVATARS', function() {
ta.retrieve('friendAvatarSwitcherObj').replaceAvatarsOnPage();
});
ta.queueForLoad(function() { // just in case we have the ta object before the DOM is fully initialized
ta.retrieve('friendAvatarSwitcherObj').findAvatarsOnPage(); // as soon as we can, start parsing the DOM for avatars

function daysSince(curr, prev) {
var current = new Date(curr.getFullYear(), curr.getMonth(), curr.getDate());
var previous = new Date(prev.getFullYear(), prev.getMonth(), prev.getDate());
var timeSince = current.getTime() - previous.getTime();
var days = timeSince / 86400000; // 86400000 milliseconds = 1 day
return Math.floor(days);
}
function isChromePluginInstalled(extensionId, installedCallback, notInstalledCallback)
{
if (chrome && chrome.runtime && chrome.runtime.sendMessage) {
chrome.runtime.sendMessage(extensionId, { message: "installed" },
function (reply) {
if (reply) {
installedCallback && installedCallback();
} else {
notInstalledCallback && notInstalledCallback();
}
}
);
} else {
notInstalledCallback();
}
}
function requestPcbVelocity(placement) {
var reqData = {
servletClass: "MetaPlacementAjax",
placementName: placement,
assets: "false",
wrap: "true",
skipLocation: "true"
}
require(['overlays/Overlay', 'overlays/styles/modal', 'overlays/position', 'overlays/options/closeOnEscape',
'overlays/options/closeOnDocClick', 'overlays/options/autoReposition', 'overlays/styles/windowshade',
'overlays/options/ajax'],
function(Overlay, Modal, Position, CloseOnEscape, CloseOnDocClick, AutoReposition, WindowShade, Ajax) {
var pcb = new Overlay(null, [
Modal(null, 'center', 'pcb', '', '', null),
Position.center([0,0]),
CloseOnEscape,
CloseOnDocClick,
AutoReposition,
WindowShade(),
Ajax('/MetaPlacementAjax', {reqParams:reqData, resources:["https://static.tacdn.com/css2/pcb_branding_interstitial_rollout_p1-v23821076790b.css"]})
]);
pcb.on('hide', function(target) {
var hideType;
if (target.trigger) {
if (target.trigger == 'doc-click') {
hideType = 'booking_interstitial' + '_exit_outside';
}
else if (target.trigger == 'close-button') {
hideType = 'booking_interstitial' + '_exit_x';
}
else {
hideType = 'booking_interstitial' + '_exit_button';
}
}
ta.remove("PCBInterstitialOpen");
ta.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign', hideType || 'booking_interstitial' + '_exit_outside', "Hotel_Review", null, true);
}).on('contentLoaded', function() {
ta.trackEventOnPage('interruption_record', 'popup', 'pcb_campaign_interstitial', 0, true);
ta.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign', 'popup', 'pcb_campaign_interstitial', 0, true);
var closeButton = ta.find('.ui_button', pcb.container);
closeButton && closeButton.addEvent('click', function(e) {
pcb.hide();
});
});
pcb.show();
ta.store("PCBInterstitialOpen", true);
setTimeout(function() {
if (pcb && pcb.isOpen()) {
ta.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign', 'booking_interstitial' + '_in_view', "Hotel_Review", null, true);
}
}, 3000);
}
);
}

function ip_adjustHeader() {
// check for overlap
var prefs = ta.id('USER_PREFS');
var head = ta.id('HEAD');
if (!prefs || !head) {
return;
}
var logo = head.getElement('.topLogo');

define("booking/common/ChildAgesSerialization", [],
function(){
var AGES_SEPARATOR = ',';
var ROOMS_SEPARATOR = ':';
var DESERIALIZE_REGEX = new RegExp(AGES_SEPARATOR+'|'+ROOMS_SEPARATOR);
function _deserializeChildren(childrenAgesStr) {
if (childrenAgesStr == null || childrenAgesStr.length == 0) {
return [];
}
return childrenAgesStr.split(DESERIALIZE_REGEX).map(function (el) {return parseInt(el,10);}).filter(function(n){return !isNaN(n);});
}
function _serializeChildren(rooms,childrenAges) {
if (childrenAges == null || childrenAges.length == 0) {
return '';
}
var childrenPerRoom = Math.floor(childrenAges.length/rooms);
var extraChildren = childrenAges.length - (childrenPerRoom * rooms);
var roomStrings = [];
var nextIndex = 0;
for (var i = 0 ; i < rooms ; ++i) {
var childrenInRoom = 0;
if (i < extraChildren) {
childrenInRoom = childrenPerRoom + 1;
} else {
childrenInRoom = childrenPerRoom;
}
if (childrenInRoom) {
var endIndex = Math.min(nextIndex + childrenInRoom, childrenAges.length);
var inRoom = childrenAges.slice(nextIndex, endIndex);
nextIndex = endIndex;
roomStrings.push(inRoom.join(AGES_SEPARATOR));
}
}
return roomStrings.join(ROOMS_SEPARATOR);
}
return {
deserialize: _deserializeChildren,
serialize: _serializeChildren
}

// Age pickers
//
//update picker text and status of a specific age picker to given age
// @param age - the new age to show
// @param agePicker - the picker to update
function _selectAgeForPicker(age, agePicker, showError) {
var error=false;
//this means age was not selected yet
if (age === -1) {
age = 'Age';//{@localize key="mem_pf_928"/} {! Age !}
error = true;
}
if (age === 0) {
age = '0-1';
}
api.find('.picker-inner .picker-label', agePicker).firstChild.nodeValue = age;
api.find('.curoption .picker-label', agePicker).firstChild.nodeValue = age;
if (!error || !showError) {
api.removeClass(api.find('.picker-inner', agePicker), 'error');
} else {
api.addClass(api.find('.picker-inner', agePicker), 'error');
}
//for removing the age-error text
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_agesPopupVerify();
} else {
_updateAgesErrorMsg(true);
}
}
//adds event listener for a specific age picker dropdown option
// @param option - the drop down element
// @param age - the age it represents
// @param agePicker - the picker adding to
function _addSelectAgeListener(option, age, agePicker) {
api.addEvent(option, 'click', function(event) {
_selectAgeForPicker(age, agePicker, true);
_showPicker(false, agePicker);
_updateGuestsRoomsObject();
event.stopPropagation();
});
}
//adds age option to a specific picker

// @param agePicker - the picker to add to
// @param optionsParent - the dropdown options parent element
function _addAgeToPicker(age, agePicker, optionsParent){
var option = new Element('li');
api.addClass(option,'option');
option.setContent(age);
_addSelectAgeListener(option, age, agePicker);
optionsParent.appendChild(option);
}
//fills the given age picker dropdown with age options
function _fillAges(agePicker) {

_addAgeToPicker('0-1', agePicker, optionsParent);
for (var i = 1 ; i <= MAX_CHILD_AGE ; ++i ) {
_addAgeToPicker("" + i, agePicker, optionsParent);
}
}
// fill the given age picker  and add it to dom
function _addAgePicker(agePicker, index) {
var childLocArr = ta.retrieve('rgPicker.nChildIndex'), // Child {0}
childStr = childLocArr && childLocArr.length > index ? childLocArr[index] : '';
var id = 'age-picker-' + index;
agePicker.id = id; //id should be enough, but ta.find does not work properly with id selector, so adding class as well
api.addClass(agePicker, id);
api.setStyle(agePicker, 'order', index); //make sure they are laid out in the correct order
var titleElement = api.find('.picker-title', agePicker);
titleElement.innerHTML = childStr;
api.addEvent(agePicker, 'click', function(event) {
_togglePicker(agePicker);
_flushScrollbar(agePicker);
event.stopPropagation();
});
_fillAges(agePicker);
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_agesPickerContainerElement.insertBefore(agePicker, _popupUpdateButton);
} else {
_agesPickerContainerElement.appendChild(agePicker);
}
}
//updates the number of age pickers according to given number of children
function _createAgePickers(nChildren, show) {
var agePicker
, i
;
//remove unneeded pickers
for (i = nChildren ; i < MAX_CHILDREN ; ++i) {
agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
if (!agePicker) {
break;
}
_agesPickerContainerElement.removeChild(agePicker);
}
for (i = 0 ; i < nChildren ; ++i) {
agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
if (agePicker) {
continue;
}
var newPicker = _agePickerTemplate.cloneNode(true);
api.removeClass(newPicker, 'hidden');
api.removeClass(newPicker, 'age-picker-template');
_addAgePicker(newPicker, (i + 1));
}
if (nChildren > 0) {
api.removeClass(_childrenAgesExplain, 'hidden');
}
else {
api.addClass(_childrenAgesExplain, 'hidden');
}
if (show && (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup)) {
_showAgePickersPopup(true, nChildren > 0);
}
}
//create age pickers with given ages
// @param childrenAges - array of age values (integer, 0-17)
function _createAgePickersWithAges(childrenAges, showErrors) {
_createAgePickers(childrenAges.length, false);
for( var i = 0 ; i < childrenAges.length ; ++i) {
var agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
_selectAgeForPicker(childrenAges[i], agePicker, showErrors);
}
}
//collects the children ages from all pickers.
// @returns - array of ages, -1 if age not selected
function _gatherChildrenAges() {
var ages = [];
for( var i = 0 ; i < MAX_CHILDREN ; ++i) {
var agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
if (!agePicker) {
break;
}
var age = parseInt(api.find('.picker-inner .picker-label', agePicker).firstChild.nodeValue, 10);
if (isNaN(age)) {
ages.push(-1);
} else {
ages.push(age);
}
}
return ages;
}
function _showAgesAsText(asText) {
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
_childrenAges = ages;
if (asText) {
var agesStrings = ages.map(function(a) { return a === 0 ? '0-1' : a; });
_childrenAgesText.innerHTML = ': ' + agesStrings.join(',') + ' ';
api.removeClass(_childrenAgesText, 'hidden');
api.removeClass(_childrenAgesChange, 'hidden');
} else if (!_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
api.addClass(_childrenAgesText, 'hidden');
api.addClass(_childrenAgesChange, 'hidden');
}
if (!_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
for (var i = 0; i < MAX_CHILDREN; ++i) {
var agePicker = api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1), _agesPickerContainerElement);
if (!agePicker) {
break;
}
if (asText) {
api.addClass(agePicker, 'hidden');
} else {
api.removeClass(agePicker, 'hidden');
}
}
}
}
function _showAgePickersInlinePopup() {
api.addClass(_agesWrapElement, 'selecting');
api.addEvent(document, 'click', _onHidePopup);
}
function _hideAgePickersInlinePopup() {
if (_agesPopupVerify()) {
api.removeClass(_agesWrapElement, 'selecting');
_showAgesAsText(true);
api.removeEvent(document, 'click', _onHidePopup);
}
}
function _showAgePickersPopup(show, hasAges) {
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
if (show && hasAges) {
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_agesPopupVerify();
api.addClass(_agesWrapElement, 'hidden');
if (!_childAgePickersPopup) {
_agesPopupInit();
}
_childAgePickersPopup.show();
_mainOverlaysArr.forEach(function (o) {
o.hide();
});
}
else if (_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
_showAgePickersInlinePopup();
}
} else if(hasAges) {
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
api.removeClass(_agesWrapElement, 'hidden');
}
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
} else {
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
api.addClass(_agesWrapElement, 'hidden');
}
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
}
}
// general
//
function _fillPickerOptions(parent, labelsName, min, max, prop, triggerSearchFirstOption, triggerSearchAll) {
var optionsParent = api.find(' .picker-dropdown .options-container', parent)
, labels = ta.retrieve(labelsName)
, option
, obj
, i
;
for ( i = min ; i <= max ; ++i ) {
option = new Element('li');
api.addClass(option, 'option');
option.setContent(labels[i]);
obj = {};
obj[prop] = i;
_addPickerListener(parent, option, obj, triggerSearchAll || (triggerSearchFirstOption && i === min));
optionsParent.appendChild(option);
}
}
function _addPickerListener(picker, option, values, triggerSearch) {
api.addEvent(option, 'click', function(event) {
var changed = _updateValues(values, true, true);
_showPicker(false, picker);
_verifyFields(false, false, true);
event.stopPropagation();
if (triggerSearch && changed) {
_doSearch(false, event);
}
});
}
function _togglePicker(parent, trk) {
//this is an overlay...
var willShow;
if (parent && parent.isOpen) {
willShow = !parent.isOpen();
} else {
var dropdown = api.find('.picker-dropdown', parent);
willShow = api.hasClass(dropdown, 'hidden');
}
_showPicker(willShow, parent);
if (trk && willShow) {
_trackEvent(trk);
}
}
function _hideChildAgePickersPopup(){
if (_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
_hideAgePickersInlinePopup();
}
else if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && _childAgePickersPopup && _childAgePickersPopup.isOpen()) {
_childAgePickersPopup.hide();
}
}
function _showPicker(show, parent) {
//close a picker if already open
var currentlyOpenDD = api.find('.picker-dropdown:not(.hidden)', _widgetDiv);
if (parent.isOpen) {
api.addClass(currentlyOpenDD, 'hidden');
if(show) {
if(!parent.isOpen()) {
_mainOverlaysArr.forEach(function(o) { o.hide(); });
}
parent.show();
//close the ages popup in case one of the main pickers is opened
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
} else {
parent.hide();
}
} else {
_mainOverlaysArr.forEach(function(o) { o.hide(); });
var dropdown = api.find('.picker-dropdown', parent);
if (currentlyOpenDD !== dropdown) {
api.addClass(currentlyOpenDD, 'hidden');
}
if (api.hasClass(dropdown, 'hidden')) {
if (show) {
api.removeClass(dropdown, 'hidden');
}
} else {
if (!show) {
api.addClass(dropdown, 'hidden');
}
}
//close the ages popup in case one of the main pickers is opened
if (show && (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) && (!api.hasClass(parent, 'age-picker'))) {
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
}
}
//one place to hold logic for all versions of the test
function _updateValues(valuesObj, show, notify) {
var nRooms = valuesObj.nRooms || _numRooms
, nAdults = valuesObj.nAdults || _numAdults
, nChildren = (typeof(valuesObj.nChildren) === 'undefined' ? _numChildren : valuesObj.nChildren)
, newNumAdults
, newNumChildren
, newNumRooms;
if (_numRooms === nRooms && _numAdults === nAdults && _numChildren === nChildren) {
return false;
}
if (nRooms !== _numRooms) {
newNumRooms = nRooms;
if (newNumRooms > nAdults) {
//at least one adult per room
newNumAdults = newNumRooms;
} else {
//no more then 4 adults per room
newNumAdults = Math.min(nRooms * MAX_ADULTS_PER_ROOM, nAdults);
}
//no more then 8 children per room.
newNumChildren = Math.min(nRooms * MAX_CHILDREN_PER_ROOM, nChildren);
} else {
//minimal number of rooms as dictated by number of adults
var adultsRequiredNumberOfRooms = Math.ceil(nAdults / MAX_ADULTS_PER_ROOM);
//but they might want more rooms
adultsRequiredNumberOfRooms = Math.max(adultsRequiredNumberOfRooms, nRooms);
//minimal number of rooms as dictated by number of children
var childrenRequiredNumberOfRooms = Math.ceil(nChildren / MAX_CHILDREN_PER_ROOM);
//maximal number of rooms required
newNumRooms = Math.max(adultsRequiredNumberOfRooms, childrenRequiredNumberOfRooms);
//at least one adult per room
newNumRooms = Math.min(newNumRooms, nAdults);
//force max children per room
newNumChildren = Math.min(nChildren, newNumRooms * MAX_CHILDREN_PER_ROOM);
newNumAdults = nAdults;
}
var changed = false;
if (newNumRooms !== _numRooms) {
_setRoomsLabel(newNumRooms);
changed = true;
}
if (newNumChildren !== _numChildren) {
_createAgePickers(newNumChildren, show);
}
if (newNumAdults !== _numAdults) {
_setAdultsLabel(newNumAdults);
changed = true;
}
if (newNumChildren !== _numChildren) {
_setChildrenLabel(newNumChildren);
changed = true;
}
_numRooms = newNumRooms;
_numAdults = newNumAdults;
_numChildren = newNumChildren;
if (notify) {
_updateGuestsRoomsObject(false);
}
return changed;
}
//handle click outside of the drop downs of the various pickers
function _closeOpenPicker(event) {
var openDD = api.find('.picker-dropdown:not(.hidden)', _widgetDiv);
api.addClass(openDD, 'hidden');
_mainOverlaysArr.forEach(function(o) {
if (!event || !o.sourceElement.contains(event.target)) {
o.hide();
}
});
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
if(!event || event.target !== _childrenAgesChange) {
_hideChildAgePickersPopup();
}
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
}
function _trackEvent(action) {
var trackingTree = '',
ik = ta.retrieve("tracking.impression.key"),
locationId = ta.retrieve('page.location');
if (ik) {
trackingTree =  "IK:" + ik;
}
if (locationId) {
trackingTree += "/L:" + locationId;
}
var context = _dynamicContext ? _detectContext() : _trackContext;
ta.trackEventOnPage('GuestSelector-'+context||'', action, trackingTree, "1", false);
}
//updates the global object with selected values
function _updateGuestsRoomsObject() {
var orig = ta.retrieve('guests.rooms.object');
var obj = {
guests:_numAdults,
rooms:_numRooms,
child_rm_ages: ser.serialize(_numRooms, _gatherChildrenAges())
};
var changed = JSON.stringify(orig) !== JSON.stringify(obj);
var curDates = JSON.stringify(_calendarProxy.getDates());
if(!changed )
{
changed = _lastKnownDates !== curDates;
}
_lastKnownDates = curDates;
if (changed) {
ta.store('guests.rooms.object', obj);
_setDirtyMode(true);
//let other children pickers know about the new values
ta.fireEvent('onLegacyGuestsChanged', obj);
if (_childAgePickersPopup) {
_childAgePickersPopup.reposition();
}
}
}
function _onSearchFieldsChanged(source){
if (source === _widgetDiv){
return;
}
var obj = ta.retrieve('guests.rooms.object');
_childrenAges = ser.deserialize(obj.child_rm_ages);
_createAgePickersWithAges(_childrenAges, false);
_setInitialState(obj.rooms, obj.guests, false);
_showAgesAsText(true);
}
function _onClearSearch() {
_updateValues( {nRooms:1, nAdults:2, nChildren:0}, true, true );
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup ) {
api.addClass(_widgetDiv, 'hidden');
}
}
function _setDirtyMode(dirty) {
_dirty = dirty;
if (_calendarProxy.hasDates()) {
if (_searchButton && _canChangeSearchButton) {
if (!_showChildrenAgesInPopup && !api.hasClass(_searchButton,'no_hide')) {
_searchButton.firstChild.nodeValue = ta.retrieve('common_update_results');//"Update Results";
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'original');
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'primary');
} else if(_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
var inner = api.find('.change_dates_text', _searchButton);
(inner || _searchButton).firstChild.nodeValue = ta.retrieve('airm_updateSearchLabel');//"Update Search";
}
}
}
if (dirty) {
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
if (!api.hasClass(_searchButton, 'no_hide')) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'hidden');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && (!_childAgePickersPopup || !_childAgePickersPopup.isOpen())) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup && !api.hasClass(_agesWrapElement, 'selecting')) {
api.removeClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
_showAgesAsText(false);
} else {
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
if (!api.hasClass(_searchButton, 'no_hide')) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'hidden');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && (!_childAgePickersPopup || !_childAgePickersPopup.isOpen())) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup && !api.hasClass(_agesWrapElement, 'selecting')) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
_showAgesAsText(true);
}
}
function _updateAgesErrorMsg(removeOnly, hasAgesError) {
var hasErrors = false;
if (typeof(hasAgesError) === "undefined") {
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
for (var i = 0; i < ages.length; ++i) {
if (ages[i] < 0) {
hasErrors = true;
}
}
} else {
hasErrors = hasAgesError;
}
if (!hasErrors) {
api.addClass(api.find('.ages-error', _agesWrapElement), 'hidden');
} else if (!removeOnly) {
_trackEvent('age_validation_error');
api.removeClass(api.find('.ages-error', _agesWrapElement), 'hidden');
}
}
//verify fields values
// @params interactive - indicated if should show visuals on errors
// @returns - boolean indicating if error was found
function _verifyFields(interactive, agesOnly, removeAgesErrorIsPossible) {
var hasErrors = false,
hasAgesError = false;
if (!_calendarProxy.hasDates()) {
if (interactive) {
_calendarProxy.showCalendar();
}
hasErrors = true;
}
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
for (var i = 0 ; i < ages.length ; ++i) {
if (ages[i] < 0) {
hasErrors = true;
hasAgesError = true;
if (interactive || agesOnly) {
api.addClass(api.find('.age-picker-' + (i + 1) + ' .picker-inner', _agesPickerContainerElement), 'error');
}
}
}
if (interactive || agesOnly) {
_updateAgesErrorMsg(false, hasAgesError);
}
if (removeAgesErrorIsPossible && !hasAgesError) {
api.addClass(api.find('.ages-error', _agesWrapElement), 'hidden');
}
return !hasErrors;
}
function _agesPopupVerify() {
var hasAgesError = false;
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
for (var i = 0 ; i < ages.length ; ++i) {
if (ages[i] < 0) {
hasAgesError = true;
break;
}
}
if (!hasAgesError) {
api.removeClass(_popupUpdateButton, 'disabled');
} else {
api.addClass(_popupUpdateButton, 'disabled');
}
return !hasAgesError;
}
function _updateSearchButtonPopupClick(event) {
if (_agesPopupVerify()) {
_showAgesAsText(true);
_showAgePickersPopup(false, _childrenAges.length > 0);
if (!_searchImmediately) { //search immediatly will trigger the search from the hide popup function, so no need to do this again
_doSearch(true, event);
}
}
}
function _doSearch(triggerDatesSelected, event) {
_closeOpenPicker();
if (!_verifyFields(true) && _canChangeSearchButton) {
return;
}
if (triggerDatesSelected && _canChangeSearchButton) {
var dates = _calendarProxy.getDates();
_calendarProxy.fireDatesChanged(dates);
}
if (typeof(_origSearchHandler) === 'function') {
_origSearchHandler.apply(_searchButton,[event]);
}
_setDirtyMode(false);
ta.fireEvent('searchFieldsChanged', _widgetDiv);
}
function _changeAgesClick(event) {
if(event) {
event.stopPropagation();
}
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
_showAgePickersPopup(true, true);
}
if (!_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_showAgesAsText(false);
}
_trackEvent('change_age_click');
}
//search button click handler
function _searchClick(event) {
event = new Event(event);
event.stop();
_trackEvent('update_results_click');
_doSearch(true, event);
}
function _onDatesChanged(sourceElement, type) {
if (! _calendarProxy.isDateTypeRelevant(type)) {
return;
}
if (api.hasClass(sourceElement, 'prw_ibex_rooms_guests_picker')  //triggered by one of the instances of this widget
|| _closestDatePickers.indexOf(sourceElement) === -1) { //triggered by a date picker of other instance
//need to hide search button
_setDirtyMode(false);
return;
}
if (!_noAutoHac) {
//search immediately when dates changed
_doSearch(false);
//show after search started. needed for the way hotels page works
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && _calendarProxy.hasDates()) {
setTimeout(function () {
api.removeClass(_widgetDiv, 'hidden');
}, 100);
}
}
}
// somewhat similar to the one in Desktop.js, but can get which picker type
function _findClosestDatepicker(type) {
var el,
target = _widgetDiv;
while (target && target !== document.body) {
el = target.getElement('[data-dateType='+type+']');
if (el) {
return el;
}
target = target.parentNode;
}
return null;
}
function _findSearchButton()
{
// looking for the relevant search button - it is located outside of the widget
// since it is implemented by the container that uses the widget.
// but this should not be too far away, so looking two levels up max.
var parent = _widgetDiv.parentNode;
for (var i = 0 ; i < 2 ; ++i) {
var button = api.find('.update_results_button', parent);
if (button) {
return button;
}
parent = parent.parentNode;
}
return null;
}
function _detectContext() {
var classStr = _widgetDiv.className.toLowerCase(),
classArray = classStr.split(' ').filter(function(s) { return s.indexOf('wctx-',0) === 0; });
if (classArray.length > 0) {
return classArray[0].substring(5);
}
}
function _commonInit() {
_searchImmediately = api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'popup_with_button');
_showChildrenAgesInPopup = _searchImmediately || api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'popup');
_showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup = api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'inline_popup');
_noAutoHac = api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'noAutoHac');
_dynamicContext = api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'dynamic_context');
_trackContext = _detectContext();
_agesWrapElement = api.find('.ages-wrap', _widgetDiv);
_agesPickerContainerElement = _showChildrenAgesInPopup ? api.find('.ages-wrap-popup-container', _widgetDiv) : _agesWrapElement;
_agePickerTemplate = api.find('.ages-wrap .age-picker-template', _widgetDiv);
_initialValuesHolder = api.find('.initial-values-holder', _widgetDiv);
_childrenAgesExplain = api.find('.children-ages-explain', _widgetDiv);
_childrenAgesChange = api.find('.ages_change', _childrenAgesExplain);
_childrenAgesText = api.find('.ages_text', _childrenAgesExplain);
_searchButton = _findSearchButton();
_canChangeSearchButton = ! api.hasClass(_searchButton,'no_change');
_numRooms = Number(_initialValuesHolder.getAttribute('numRooms'));
_numAdults = Number(_initialValuesHolder.getAttribute('numAdults'));
_childrenAgesStr = _initialValuesHolder.getAttribute('childrenAges');
_closestDatePickers = [_findClosestDatepicker('CHECKIN'), _findClosestDatepicker('CHECKOUT')];
if (_searchButton) {
_origSearchHandler = _searchButton.onclick;
_searchButton.onclick = _searchClick;
}
_childrenAgesChange.onclick = _changeAgesClick;
_calendarProxy.onDatesSelected(_onDatesChanged);
ta.on('searchFieldsChanged', _onSearchFieldsChanged);
ta.on('childrenClearSearch', _onClearSearch);
_childrenAges = ser.deserialize(_childrenAgesStr);
_createAgePickersWithAges(_childrenAges, true);
api.addEvent(document, 'click', _closeOpenPicker);
_lastKnownDates = JSON.stringify(_calendarProxy.getDates());
}
function _flushScrollbar(parentElement) {
if(!parentElement) {
return;
}
var scrollContainer = api.find('.options-container', parentElement);
if(!scrollContainer) {
return;
}
//on mac, this will animate the scroll bar so the user knows it can be scrolled
scrollContainer.scrollTop = scrollContainer.scrollTop + 1;
scrollContainer.scrollTop = scrollContainer.scrollTop - 1;
}
function _pickerClick(event, pickerElement, overlay, pickerTrack) {
if (!overlay) {
overlay = _setupDropdown(pickerElement, pickerTrack);
_mainOverlaysArr.push(overlay);
}
_togglePicker(overlay, pickerTrack);
_flushScrollbar(api.find('.picker-dropdown', overlay.container));
return overlay;
}
function _setupDropdown(pickerElement, pickerTrack) {
var dropdown = null;
var content = api.find('.picker-dropdown', pickerElement);
api.removeClass(content, 'hidden');
var size = api.getSize(pickerElement);
var dropdownStyle = 'border: 1px solid #589442;border-radius: 3px;padding:0;';
dropdown = new Overlay(
pickerElement,
Dropdown(pickerElement, 'below', [_widgetDiv.get('class')], content, dropdownStyle, 'div'),
Position.below([0, -(size.y || 36)]),
MatchWidth && MatchWidth(pickerElement),
CloseOnDocClick,
CloseOnLegacyOverlay,
CloseOnTargetEvent(window, ['date_bar_docked', 'date_bar_undocked'])
);
api.removeClass(dropdown.contentElement, 'hidden');
api.find('.curoption', dropdown.container).onclick = function(event) {
_togglePicker(dropdown, pickerTrack);
_flushScrollbar(content);
event.stopPropagation();
};
return dropdown;
}
function _hrInit() {
_roomsElement = api.find('.rooms-picker .unified-picker', _widgetDiv);
_adultsElement = api.find('.adults-picker .unified-picker', _widgetDiv);
_childrenElement = api.find('.children-picker .unified-picker', _widgetDiv);
_fillRoomsOptions();
_fillAdultsOptions();
_fillChildrenOptions();
_roomsElement.onclick = function(event) { _roomsOverlay = _pickerClick(event, _roomsElement, _roomsOverlay, 'room_picker_open'); };
_adultsElement.onclick = function(event) { _adultsOverlay = _pickerClick(event, _adultsElement, _adultsOverlay, 'adult_picker_open'); };
_childrenElement.onclick = function(event) { _childrenOverlay = _pickerClick(event, _childrenElement, _childrenOverlay, 'children_picker_open'); };
}
function _onHidePopup() {
//remove children which for age was not picked.
var ages = _gatherChildrenAges();
ages = ages.filter(function(a){ return a >= 0; });
_updateValues({nChildren:ages.length}, true, true);
_createAgePickersWithAges(ages, false);
_showAgesAsText(true);
_showAgePickersPopup(false, ages.length > 0);
if (_dirty) {
_doSearch(false);
}
}
function _agesPopupInit() {
_popupUpdateButton = api.find('.update_search_button', _agesPickerContainerElement );
_popupUpdateButton.onclick = _updateSearchButtonPopupClick;
if (_searchImmediately) {
api.removeClass(_popupUpdateButton, 'hidden');
}
api.removeClass(_agesPickerContainerElement, 'hidden');
_childAgePickersPopup = new Overlay(
_childrenElement,
Tooltip(_childrenElement, 'below', [_widgetDiv.get('class')], _agesPickerContainerElement, 'div'),
Position.below(),
CloseOnDocClick,
CloseOnLegacyOverlay,
CloseOnTargetEvent(window, ['date_bar_docked', 'date_bar_undocked'])
);
api.removeClass(_childAgePickersPopup.container,'hidden');
_childAgePickersPopup.on('hide', _onHidePopup);
}
//init the components with given rooms/adults/children values.
function _setInitialState(nRooms, nAdults, notify) {
_updateValues({ nRooms:nRooms || _numRooms, nAdults:nAdults || _numAdults, nChildren:_childrenAges.length }, false, notify);
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup) {
_showAgePickersPopup(false, _childrenAges.length > 0);
}
if (_verifyFields(false)) {
if (_canChangeSearchButton) {
if (!api.hasClass(_searchButton, 'no_hide')) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'hidden');
} else if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup || _showChildrenAgesInInlinePopup) {
api.addClass(_searchButton, 'disabled');
}
}
_showAgesAsText(true);
} else {
_showAgesAsText(false);
}
if (_showChildrenAgesInPopup && !api.hasClass(_widgetDiv, 'no_hide')) {
if (_calendarProxy.hasDates()) {
api.removeClass(_widgetDiv, 'hidden');
} else {
api.addClass(_widgetDiv, 'hidden');
}
}
}
function _setupCalendarProxy() {
if (ta.page && ta.page.getDates) {
_calendarProxy = {
hasDates: function() { return ta.page.hasDates('STAYDATES'); },
getDates: function() { return ta.page.getDates('STAYDATES'); },
showCalendar: function() { ta.page.gatherDatesNear(event.target, null, false); },
fireDatesChanged: function(dates) { ta.page.onDatesSelected(_closestDatePickers[0], 'STAYDATES', dates, true); },
onDatesSelected: function(callback) { ta.page.on('dateSelected', callback); },
isDateTypeRelevant: function(type) { return type === 'STAYDATES'; }
};
} else if(ta.widgets && ta.widgets.calendar) {
_calendarProxy = {
hasDates: function() { return ta.widgets.calendar.hasPageDates(); },
getDates: function() { return ta.widgets.calendar.getDateArgsObject(); },
showCalendar: function() { },
fireDatesChanged: function(/* dates */) { ta.widgets.calendar.updateSDCalendar(); },
onDatesSelected: function(callback) { ta.on('onCalendarRangeSelect', callback); },
isDateTypeRelevant: function(/* type */) { return true; }
};
}
}
//init the widget
function _init(){
_setupCalendarProxy();
_commonInit();
if (ta.retrieve('feature.CHILDREN_SEARCH'))
{
_hrInit();
}
if (ta.retrieve('guests.rooms.object')) {
//this is a widget refresh, take values from ta to keep in sync with other instances
_onSearchFieldsChanged();
} else {
//this is the first render - take values from default fields
_setInitialState(null,null,true);
}
}
ta.queueForLoad(function() {
_init();
}, 'rooms and guests picker widget handlers');
});

'use strict';

function _onDateSelected(target, dateType, date) {
// Clean up if the widget is no longer in the document.
if (!ta.inDocument(widget.element)) {
ta.page.removeListener('dateSelected', _onDateSelected);
_checkinElement = null;
_checkoutElement = null;
return;
}
if (dateType === 'CHECKIN') {
_setDateLabel(_checkinElement, date[0]);
} else if (dateType === 'CHECKOUT') {
_setDateLabel(_checkoutElement, date[0]);
} else if (dateType === 'STAYDATES') {
_setDateLabel(_checkinElement, date[0]);
_setDateLabel(_checkoutElement, date[1]);
}
}
/* HOT-4552 */
function _onDatePickerClick(elmt) {
if (!elmt) {
return;
}
var calendarFlyout = elmt.getParent(".calendarFlyout");
if (calendarFlyout) {
var deferred = calendarFlyout.retrieve('deferred'),
calendarWrapper = calendarFlyout.getElement('.calendarWrapper');
if (deferred && calendarWrapper) {
deferred.reject();
ta.page.gatherDates(elmt, calendarWrapper);
return;
}
}
ta.page.gatherDates(elmt);
}
ta.queueForLoad(function() {
ta.page.on('dateSelected', _onDateSelected);
}, 'datepicker widget handlers');
return {
onDatePickerClick: _onDatePickerClick
};
